function
deleteConfirm(
obj,
url
)
{




var
confirmed
=
confirm('Are
you
sure
you
want
to
delete
this
list?');

(confirmed)

{

false;




}


}

<script>


function
cdLLFailure(divErrorID,
divLoadID)
{




jQuery(divErrorID).css('display',
'');




jQuery(divLoadID).remove();


}


function
cdLLSuccess(response,
divErrorID,
divLoadID,
divContentID)
{




if
(response.hasError)
{






if
(response.content.length
>
0)
{








jQuery(divErrorID).html(response.content);






}






cdLLFailure(divErrorID,
divLoadID);




}
else
{






jQuery(divContentID).html(response.content);




}


}


function
cdLLHandler(masterID,
handlerURL,
handlerArgs,
activationRange,
timeout)
{




var
divContentID
=
masterID
+
'Content';




var
divLoadID



=
masterID
+
'Loading';




var
divErrorID


=
masterID
+
'Error';





if
(window.cdLLoading[masterID])






return;





var
winPositionY
=
jQuery(window).scrollTop()
+
jQuery(window).height();




var
elementFound
=
jQuery(divContentID).size();




var
divPositionY
=
jQuery(divContentID).offset().top;





if
(elementFound
&&
(
divPositionY
-
winPositionY
<
activationRange
))
{






window.cdLLoading[masterID]
=
true;






jQuery.ajax({








url





:
handlerURL,








cache



:
false,








timeout

:
timeout,








dataType
:
"json",








data




:
handlerArgs,








error



:
function()
{cdLLFailure(divErrorID,
divLoadID)},








success

:
function(response)
{cdLLSuccess(response,
divErrorID,
divLoadID,
divContentID)}






});




}


}
</script>
